## 4. TERMINAL IDENTITY, OWNERSHIP, AND AUTHORIZATION VALIDATION

### 4a. Terminal Identity — `TerminalRequestFilter.java`

The `TerminalRequestFilter` (a `OncePerRequestFilter`) runs AFTER `JwtRequestFilter` in the security chain (configured in `SecurityConfig.java` line 155). It:

1. Reads the `X-Terminal-Token` header
2. Validates the token type is `"terminal"` (via `jwtUtility.extractTokenType()`)
3. Cross-checks the `restaurantId` claim against `TenantContext.getCurrentTenant()` (set by JWT auth)
4. Extracts `terminalId`, `terminalSeries`, `deviceId`, `credVer` from the token
5. **Credential version verification**:
   - If the token has `credVer`, it must match the DB `credential_version` exactly (rejects both older and future versions)
   - If the token lacks `credVer` (legacy), it's only accepted if the terminal's DB `credential_version` is still 1 (never rotated)
6. **Status check**: Rejects tokens for non-ACTIVE terminals (reports the actual status)
7. On success, populates `TenantContext` with terminal identity:
   - `setCurrentTerminalId(terminalId)`
   - `setCurrentTerminalSeries(terminalSeries)`
   - `setCurrentTerminalDevice(deviceId)`
   - `setCurrentTerminalActive(true)`

### 4b. Terminal Ownership Validation — `BillTerminalUtil.java`

Pure helper class that determines whether a terminal can modify a bill:

- `ownerTerminalId(bill)`: Returns `currentOwnerTerminalId` falling back to `createdTerminalId`
- `isLegacyUnresolved(bill)`: Checks if owner is the sentinel value `"LEGACY_UNRESOLVED"`
- `isFinalized(bill)`: Bills with order status `completed`/`paid`/`cancelled`, or with a positive `refundAmount`, or from online sources (`zomato`/`swiggy`/`own_website`) are immutable
- `isModifiableByTerminal(parent, trustedTerminalId, trustedDeviceId, isAdmin)`:
  - Finalized bills → not modifiable (unless admin or owning terminal — see GenericSyncService)
  - Admin → always modifiable
  - No owner (null) → modifiable (pre-terminal compatibility)
  - `LEGACY_UNRESOLVED` → only modifiable by the original device that created it (matched by `createdDeviceId`)
  - No `trustedTerminalId` → modifiable (legacy no-token client, only when `terminal.sync.strict=false`)
  - Otherwise → must match owner exactly

### 4c. Terminal Authorization in Sync — `GenericSyncService.java`

On every push sync (lines 157–199):

1. If a terminal token is present (`TenantContext.getCurrentTerminalId()` or `getCurrentTerminalSeries()` is non-null):
   - Looks up the `RestaurantTerminal` by series or ID
   - Rejects if terminal not found or not active
   - Sets `trustedTerminalId`, `trustedTerminalSeries`, `trustedDeviceId`
2. **Strict mode** (`terminal.sync.strict=true`): If no terminal token on a transactional payload (`Bill`, `BillItem`, `BillPayment`) and caller is not admin, rejects with 400
3. **Bill pushes** (lines 278–300): Overwrites all client-sent terminal fields (`terminalId`, `terminalSeries`, `createdDeviceId`, `deviceId`, `createdTerminalId`, `currentOwnerTerminalId`) from the trusted terminal context
4. **Existing bill updates** (lines 356–385): Checks `BillTerminalUtil.ownerTerminalId()` — if another terminal owns the bill:
   - `LEGACY_UNRESOLVED` bills: only the original tablet (by `createdDeviceId`) + admin can touch them
   - Otherwise: cross-terminal updates are rejected
5. **Child record ownership** (BillItem/BillPayment, lines 442–455, 522–536): Enforces parent-bill terminal ownership — one terminal cannot attach child records to another terminal's bill
6. **Owner-only finalized bill access** (lines 709–718): A finalized bill is immutable for other terminals, but the owning terminal (or admin) can still attach finalizing payments/items

### 4d. Terminal Authorization in Master Pull — `MasterSyncController.java`

- Lines 84–115: Terminal identity comes from `X-Terminal-Token` (set by `TerminalRequestFilter` into `TenantContext`), NEVER from the client query parameter
- If a client-supplied `terminalId` differs from the authenticated terminal → **403 Forbidden**
- **Compatibility mode** (`terminal.sync.compatibility=true`): Falls back to client-supplied terminalId when no token is present
- **Strict mode** (`terminal.sync.strict=true` or compatibility disabled): Requires terminal identity for bill pulls; rejects non-admin with 400
- Bill/Item/Payment pull filtering: When `effectiveTerminalId` is set, pulls only records where `createdTerminalId = :terminalId OR currentOwnerTerminalId = :terminalId` (via `findUpdatedForTerminal` queries in Bill/BillItem/BillPayment repositories)

### 4e. Access Control via Security Config (`SecurityConfig.java`)

- `/sync/terminal/**` → `hasAnyRole("OWNER", "SHOP_ADMIN")` (line 139)
- `/business/terminals/**`, `/business/terminal-requests/**` → `hasAnyRole("OWNER", "SHOP_ADMIN")` (line 134)
- `/business/**` (other business APIs) → `hasRole("OWNER")` (line 137)
- `@RequireRole(UserRole.OWNER)` on individual web admin endpoints for additional granularity
- `/sync/**` (general sync) → `hasRole("OWNER")` (line 146)
- `POST /business/terminals/{terminalId}/reactivate` → `@RequireRole({OWNER, SHOP_ADMIN})` (line 127 of BusinessAdminController)

---

## 5. TERMINAL ACTIVATION / DEACTIVATION

### Activation Paths

There are **five** distinct paths to activate a terminal:

#### Path 1: First-ever terminal (OWNER auto-create)
- Endpoint: `POST /sync/terminal/activate` (Case 4)
- Condition: Restaurant has ZERO terminals, caller is `OWNER`
- Uses `lockRestaurantForTerminalOp()` to acquire pessimistic lock on restaurant profile
- Double-checks after lock (race-lost guard)
- Creates terminal with series `"A"`, name `"Terminal A"`, deviceId from request, status `"ACTIVE"`, credentialVersion `1L`
- Returns full `TerminalActivationResponse` including a fresh terminal token

#### Path 2: Known device with valid terminal token (re-authentication)
- Endpoint: `POST /sync/terminal/activate` (Case 1b)
- Condition: DeviceId matches an existing terminal, AND caller presents a valid terminal token for that same device
- Updates `updatedAt` heartbeat timestamp
- Returns terminal credentials

#### Path 3: Known device, no token (reinstall recovery)
- Endpoint: `POST /sync/terminal/activate` (Case 1c)
- Condition: DeviceId matches an existing terminal, but no valid token
- **Fast path**: If there's already an APPROVED request for this device, return credentials directly (handles app restart after approval)
- Otherwise: Creates a `RECOVERY` registration request → admin must approve
- Returns `PENDING_APPROVAL` status

#### Path 4: Unknown device (new terminal registration)
- Endpoint: `POST /sync/terminal/activate` (Case 2)
- Condition: DeviceId not found, no existing terminals match
- Creates a `NEW_DEVICE` registration request → admin must approve
- Respects 5-minute rejection cooldown

#### Path 5: Admin approve
- Endpoint: `POST /business/terminal-requests/{requestId}/approve`
- Locks the request row (pessimistic) and restaurant profile row
- For `RECOVERY`/`REPLACEMENT`: rebinds existing terminal, sets ACTIVE, increments credentialVersion
- For `NEW_DEVICE`: allocates next series via `allocateNextSeries()`, creates new terminal with credentialVersion 1
- Both: marks request APPROVED, assigns terminal, issues token
- Returns terminal info (series, name, status)

### Deactivation

- Endpoint: `POST /business/terminals/{terminalId}/deactivate`
- Service: `TerminalManagementService.deactivateTerminal()`
- Validates terminal exists and belongs to restaurant
- Checks terminal is currently ACTIVE (rejects if already INACTIVE)
- Sets `status = "INACTIVE"`, `isActive = false`, increments `credentialVersion` (revokes all issued tokens)
- Audits: `TERMINAL_DEACTIVATED`

### Reactivation

- Endpoint: `POST /business/terminals/{terminalId}/reactactivate`
- Service: `BusinessWriteService.reactivateTerminal()`
- Locks restaurant profile for atomic limit check
- Validates terminal exists and is currently INACTIVE
- Enforces 5-terminal limit
- Sets `status = "ACTIVE"`, `isActive = true`, increments `credentialVersion`
- Also available through `TerminalManagementService.recoverTerminal()` which handles INACTIVE → ACTIVE transition (including limit check)

### Recovery (rebind to new device)

- Endpoints:
  - `POST /sync/terminal/reclaim` (Android, post-reinstall)
  - `POST /business/terminals/{terminalId}/recover` (Web admin)
- Core implementation: `TerminalManagementService.recoverTerminal()`
- Locks restaurant profile
- Validates recovery eligibility: `ACTIVE`, `INACTIVE`, and `RECOVERY_REQUIRED` are eligible; `REVOKED` and `REPLACED` are not
- Idempotent: if already bound to same device and ACTIVE, does not rotate
- If transitioning from non-ACTIVE to ACTIVE, enforces 5-terminal limit
- Sets new `deviceId`, sets `status = "ACTIVE"`, increments `credentialVersion`
- Issues fresh terminal token

---

## 6. DEVICE REGISTRATION REQUESTS (APPROVE / REJECT)

### Entity: `DeviceRegistrationRequest.java`
- **Table**: `device_registration_request`
- **Statuses**: `PENDING` → `APPROVED` / `REJECTED` / `EXPIRED`
- **Request types**: `NEW_DEVICE`, `RECOVERY`, `REPLACEMENT`
- **Key columns**: `restaurant_id`, `device_id`, `request_type`, `status`, `matched_terminal_id` (for RECOVERY/REPLACEMENT), `assigned_terminal_id` (set after approval), `rejection_reason`

### Repository: `DeviceRegistrationRequestRepository.java`
- `findByRestaurantIdAndStatusOrderByRequestedAtDesc()` — list by status
- `findByRestaurantIdOrderByRequestedAtDesc()` — list all
- `findByRestaurantIdAndDeviceIdAndStatus()` — check for existing PENDING (dedup)
- `findMostRecentByRestaurantIdAndDeviceId()` — cooldown/reuse check
- `findByIdWithLock(id)` — pessimistic write lock for atomic approval/rejection

### Request Creation: `createOrReuseRegistrationRequest()`

Idempotent creation:
1. If a PENDING request already exists for this (restaurant, device), return it
2. If the most recent request for this device was **REJECTED** within the last 5 minutes, return null (cooldown)
3. Otherwise create and return a new PENDING request

### Approval Flow: `approveRequest()`

1. Lock the request row (pessimistic write)
2. Verify request is PENDING (reject if already processed)
3. Lock restaurant profile (serializes concurrent approvals)
4. If RECOVERY/REPLACEMENT: rebind existing terminal, handling inactive→active limit check
5. If NEW_DEVICE: check 5-terminal limit → allocate new series → create new terminal
6. Mark request APPROVED, set `assignedTerminalId`, `processedAt`, `processedByUserId`
7. Issue terminal token via `jwtUtility.generateTerminalToken()`
8. Audit: `TERMINAL_APPROVED`

### Rejection Flow: `rejectRequest()`

1. Lock the request row
2. Verify PENDING
3. Set status REJECTED, `processedAt`, `processedByUserId`, `rejectionReason`
4. Audit: `TERMINAL_REJECTED`

### Complete Activation (Android side): `POST /sync/terminal/complete-activation`

After approval, the device calls this endpoint to claim credentials:
1. Validates request is APPROVED
2. **Device binding**: Caller's deviceId must match the request's deviceId (proves same installation)
3. Verifies the assigned terminal exists, is active, and is bound to the same deviceId
4. Returns terminal credentials (including token) — idempotent

### Request Status Polling: `GET /sync/terminal/request-status/{requestId}`

Returns status + human-readable message. Does NOT return credentials (security). When APPROVED, client must call complete-activation.

---

## 7. TERMINAL SERIES ALLOCATION

### Algorithm: `TerminalManagementService.allocateNextSeries()`

```java
private String allocateNextSeries(Long restaurantId) {
    List<RestaurantTerminal> all = terminalRepository.findByRestaurantIdOrderByIdAsc(restaurantId);
    Set<String> assigned = new HashSet<>();
    for (RestaurantTerminal t : all) {
        assigned.add(t.getTerminalSeries().toUpperCase());
    }
    int n = 1;
    while (true) {
        String candidate = n <= 26 ? String.valueOf((char) ('A' + n - 1)) : "T" + n;
        if (!assigned.contains(candidate)) return candidate;
        n++;
    }
}
```

Rules:
- Series are **single uppercase letters**: `A`, `B`, `C`, ... `Z`
- After exhausting `A`–`Z`, continues with `T1`, `T2`, `T3`, ... (terminal overflow)
- First-ever terminal always gets `"A"` (hardcoded in `TerminalController.activate()` Case 4)
- The series is used for **invoice number allocation**:
  - Format: `{financialYear}{terminalSeries}{sequence}` (e.g., `24A000001`)
  - `BillServiceImpl.allocateMissingInvoiceNumbers()` locks the terminal row (`findAndLockByRestaurantIdAndTerminalSeries`) to serialize sequence allocation
  - Gated: invoices are only minted if the terminal exists (the `findAndLock...` returns a row); if the terminal doesn't exist, no invoice is allocated

---

## 8. TERMINAL TOKEN LIFECYCLE SUMMARY

| Stage | What happens | File |
|---|---|---|
| **Issuance** | `jwtUtility.generateTerminalToken()` creates a JWT with claims: `tokenType=terminal`, `terminalId`, `terminalSeries`, `deviceId`, `credVer`, `restaurantId`, `role`, `expiration` (default 30 days) | `JwtUtility.java:134` |
| **Sending** | Client receives the token in `TerminalActivationResponse.terminalToken` and sends it via `X-Terminal-Token` header on subsequent requests | `TerminalController.java:456` |
| **Validation** | `TerminalRequestFilter` validates on every request: token type, restaurant match, credential version match, terminal ACTIVE status | `TerminalRequestFilter.java` |
| **Revocation** | Any write to `credential_version` (deactivation, recovery, reactivation, reclaim) invalidates all previously-issued tokens | `TerminalManagementService.java` and `BusinessWriteService.java` |
| **Expiry** | Tokens expire after `jwt.terminal.expiration.ms` (default 30 days), checked by JWT library | `JwtUtility.java:30` |

### The `credential_version` mechanism:

- Each terminal starts at `credential_version = 1`
- Any lifecycle operation that should invalidate existing tokens increments this value:
  - `deactivateTerminal()` → +1
  - `recoverTerminal()` → +1 (unless idempotent)
  - `reclaim()` → +1 (via recoverTerminal)
  - `reactivateTerminal()` → +1
  - `approveRequest()` for RECOVERY → +1
- `TerminalRequestFilter` compares the token's `credVer` claim against the DB value:
  - Must match **exactly**
  - Legacy tokens (no credVer) only accepted if DB `credential_version` is still 1
- This means after deactivation/recovery, ALL previously-issued tokens are instantly invalid

---

## 9. TERMINAL LIMIT ENFORCEMENT

- **Hard limit**: `MAX_ACTIVE_TERMINALS = 5` (constant in `TerminalManagementService.java:31`)
- Checked in:
  - `approveRequest()`: When creating a new terminal or recovering a non-ACTIVE terminal
  - `recoverTerminal()`: When transitioning from INACTIVE to ACTIVE
  - `reactivateTerminal()` in `BusinessWriteService`: Reactivating a deactivated terminal
- All enforce by atomically counting `countByRestaurantIdAndStatus(restaurantId, "ACTIVE")` AFTER locking the restaurant profile row (`RestaurantProfileRepository.findAndLockByRestaurantId()`), ensuring serialized count checks
- When limit is hit: returns HTTP 409 `CONFLICT` with `"TERMINAL_LIMIT_REACHED"` or `"MAX_ACTIVE_TERMINALS_REACHED"`
</task_result>

## Terminal Lifecycle Analysis — Android Side

### 1. SessionManager (Terminal Identity Management)

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\domain\manager\SessionManager.kt`

**How terminal identity is stored:**
- Terminal identity is persisted across two SharedPreferences stores:
  - `session_prefs` (plain): holds `terminal_id`, `terminal_series`, `terminal_name`, `terminal_active` (boolean), `terminal_registered_at`, `terminal_last_verified_at` — all scoped by `restaurantId` (keys look like `terminal_id_<restaurantId>`).
  - `secure_session_prefs` (keystore-backed): holds `terminal_token` (scoped by `restaurantId`).
- All terminal getters (`getTerminalId()`, `getTerminalSeries()`, `getTerminalName()`, `isTerminalReady()`) return `null` if `restaurantId <= 0L`.
- `getTerminalIdentity()` assembles a `TerminalIdentity` data class from all the above prefs.
- `isTerminalReady()` checks `identity.isActive && identity.deviceId == getDeviceId()`.

**Key methods:**
- `saveTerminalIdentity(identity)` — writes all terminal fields to prefs atomically.
- `clearSession()` — removes `terminal_token` from secure prefs and clears all shared prefs. Used on hard logout.
- `clearAuthOnly()` — does NOT clear terminal identity; only clears auth token and user session (for soft re-login where terminal is preserved).

---

### 2. TerminalIdentity Model

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\domain\model\TerminalIdentity.kt`

```kotlin
data class TerminalIdentity(
    val restaurantId: Long,
    val terminalId: String,
    val deviceId: String,
    val terminalName: String?,
    val terminalSeries: String,
    val isActive: Boolean,
    val registeredAt: Long?,
    val lastVerifiedAt: Long?,
    val terminalToken: String? = null
)
```

- `terminalId`: The server-assigned unique terminal identifier (UUID string).
- `terminalSeries`: A human-readable series like "A", "B", "C1", etc. Used for display IDs and invoice series.
- `terminalToken`: A secure token issued by the server during activation; sent as `X-Terminal-Token` header on all API requests (via `AuthInterceptor`). This is what proves terminal ownership on the server side.

---

### 3. Activation Flow (SyncManager.ensureTerminalActivated)

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\domain\manager\SyncManager.kt` (lines 68-150)

**Trigger:** Called at the start of every `performMasterPull()` and `performFullSync()` cycle, before any push or pull occurs.

**What it does:**
1. Checks `sessionManager.isTerminalReady()`. If already active, returns immediately.
2. If NOT ready, calls `POST /api/v1/sync/terminal/activate` with `TerminalActivationRequest(deviceId, deviceModel)`.
3. Handles HTTP responses:
   - **200/201 (Success):** Parses `TerminalActivationResponse`, saves identity via `sessionManager.saveTerminalIdentity()`. The response supplies: `terminalId`, `terminalName`, `terminalSeries`, `isActive`, `registeredAt`, `lastVerifiedAt`, `terminalToken`.
   - **202 (Pending Approval):** Parses `TerminalPendingResponse` with `requestId` and `message`. Throws `TerminalPendingApprovalException(requestId)`.
   - **401:** Throws `HttpException` (rethrows to caller).
   - **403 (Deactivated):** Throws `IllegalStateException("Terminal has been deactivated by admin")`.
   - **429 (Rejection Cooldown):** Throws `TerminalPendingApprovalException(rejectionCooldown=true)`.
   - **Other:** Throws `HttpException`.

**Fallback for terminalId:** If `terminalId` is blank in the response, the code falls back to `terminalSeries` as the terminal identifier (line 88-89).

---

### 4. Two-Phase Activation via InitialSyncViewModel + InitialSyncScreen

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\ui\viewmodel\InitialSyncViewModel.kt`

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\ui\screens\InitialSyncScreen.kt`

**Phase 1 — Initial sync attempt:**
- On init, calls `startInitialSync()` which delegates to `syncManager.performFullSync()`.
- `performFullSync()` internally calls `ensureTerminalActivated()`.
- If the server returns 202 (pending approval), the state goes to `InitialSyncState.PendingApproval(requestId)`.

**Phase 2 — Polling for approval:**
- The `InitialSyncScreen` shows a "Waiting for Approval" UI with a Lottie animation.
- A `LaunchedEffect` polls every 15 seconds: calls `viewModel.pollRequestStatus()`.
- `pollRequestStatus()` calls `GET /api/v1/sync/terminal/request-status/{requestId}`.
- Response status handling:
  - **APPROVED:** Calls `completeActivation(requestId)`.
  - **REJECTED:** Shows error.
  - **EXPIRED:** Shows error.
  - **PENDING:** No state change (waits for next poll).

**Phase 3 — Complete activation:**
- `completeActivation()` calls `POST /api/v1/sync/terminal/complete-activation` with `CompleteActivationRequest(requestId, deviceId)`.
- On success, receives a new `TerminalActivationResponse` containing the full terminal identity including `terminalToken`.
- Calls `sessionManager.saveTerminalIdentity()` and then retries `startInitialSync()`.

**State machine:** `Idle → Syncing → (Success | PendingApproval | SessionExpired | Error)`

---

### 5. AuthInterceptor — Terminal Token on Every Request

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\data\remote\interceptor\AuthInterceptor.kt`

- On every API request (except public auth paths), adds:
  - `X-Device-Id`: device UUID
  - `Authorization: Bearer <jwt>`: auth token
  - `X-Terminal-Token`: the `terminalToken` from `sessionManager.getTerminalIdentity()` (lines 41-44)
- The server uses the terminal token to validate bill ownership and terminal binding.
- On 401, clears the auth session (but NOT the terminal identity).

---

### 6. Bill Ownership Fields

**Entity:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\data\local\entity\BillEntity.kt`

Bill entity has three terminal ownership columns:
- **`terminal_id`** — The terminal that last modified this bill (nullable, defaults to NULL).
- **`created_terminal_id`** — The terminal that created this bill (never changes after creation).
- **`current_owner_terminal_id`** — The terminal that currently "owns" this bill (may be transferred). Falls back to `created_terminal_id` on pull.

**How ownership is set during bill creation** (in `BillingViewModel`):

All three bill creation methods (`createDraftOnlineBill`, `completeOrder`, `saveDraft`) set terminal identity identically (example from `completeOrder`, lines 769-807):

```kotlin
val bill = BillEntity(
    terminalId = terminalIdentity.terminalId,
    createdTerminalId = terminalIdentity.terminalId,
    createdDeviceId = terminalIdentity.deviceId,
    currentOwnerTerminalId = terminalIdentity.terminalId,
    terminalSeries = terminalSeries,
    // ...
)
```

**Additional fields:**
- `recordOrigin`: `"local_created"` for new bills, `"server_imported"` for pulled bills, `"marketplace_imported"` for marketplace orders.
- `recordScope`: `"terminal_operational"` for mutable bills, `"restaurant_history"` for read-only history, `"restaurant_shared"` for marketplace orders.

---

### 7. Terminal Scope in Bill Queries (BillRepository.currentTerminalScope)

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\data\repository\BillRepository.kt` (lines 33-36)

```kotlin
private fun currentTerminalScope(): String =
    sessionManager.getTerminalId()
        ?: sessionManager.getTerminalSeries()
        ?: "LEGACY_UNRESOLVED"
```

This is the fallback chain used for ALL database queries that scope bills by terminal. It prefers `terminalId` (the server-assigned UUID), falls back to `terminalSeries`, and finally uses `"LEGACY_UNRESOLVED"` for pre-migration bills.

Every bill query in `BillRepository` passes the result of `currentTerminalScope()` to the DAO, which filters by `created_terminal_id = :terminalId` or `current_owner_terminal_id = :terminalId`.

**Ownership isolation (defense-in-depth):** The DAO's `getOperationalBillById` (lines 128-136 of BillDao) filters:
```sql
WHERE id = :id AND restaurant_id = :restaurantId AND is_deleted = 0
  AND (current_owner_terminal_id = :terminalId
       OR (current_owner_terminal_id IS NULL AND created_terminal_id = :terminalId))
  AND (source_channel IS NULL OR source_channel NOT IN ('zomato', 'swiggy', 'own_website'))
```

All mutation methods in `BillRepository` use `getOperationalBillById` + `isLocallyOwned()` check before allowing writes.

---

### 8. MasterSyncProcessor — Terminal-Related Push/Pull Logic

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\domain\manager\MasterSyncProcessor.kt`

**Pull (insertMasterData):**
- Bills from server carry `createdTerminalId`, `currentOwnerTerminalId`, `terminalId`, `terminalSeries`, `deviceId`.
- On pull, `createdTerminalId` falls back to `terminalId` if blank (line 914-915).
- `currentOwnerTerminalId` falls back to `createdTerminalId` if blank (line 958-960).
- `recordOrigin` and `recordScope` are set based on:
  - Draft status + matching terminal → keep `local_created`/`terminal_operational`
  - Marketplace channels → `marketplace_imported`/`restaurant_shared`
  - Otherwise → `server_imported`/`restaurant_history`
- Post-pull, `reconcileLocalBillScope()` is called to re-label this terminal's own bills.

**Post-pull reconciliation (`reconcileLocalBillScope`, lines 132-155):**
- Uses `billDao.reconcileLocalRecordScope()` to re-label synced bills back to `local_created`/`terminal_operational` for this terminal.
- Seeds `terminal_daily_counter` from the max existing local daily order ID for today — prevents duplicate order numbers after APK update/migration.

**Push (pushAll):**
- Bills are pushed as `BillSyncDto` which includes `terminalId`, `createdTerminalId`, `createdDeviceId`, `currentOwnerTerminalId`, `terminalSeries`, `operationId`.
- The DTO mapper (`BillEntity.toSyncDto()`) copies all terminal fields directly from the entity.

---

### 9. Terminal Daily Counter (Order Number Isolation)

**Entity:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\data\local\entity\TerminalDailyCounterEntity.kt`

**Primary key:** `(restaurant_id, terminal_id, date)`

This table provides per-terminal, per-day order number sequencing. Each terminal gets its own counter, so two terminals in the same restaurant have independent daily order sequences.

**Atomic increment** (in `RestaurantDao`, lines 153-161):
```sql
INSERT INTO terminal_daily_counter (restaurant_id, terminal_id, date, ...)
VALUES (:restaurantId, :terminalId, :date, 1, ...)
ON CONFLICT(restaurant_id, terminal_id, date)
DO UPDATE SET daily_order_counter = daily_order_counter + 1, ...
```

**Counter raising** (post-pull/migration seed):
```sql
INSERT ... VALUES (:restaurantId, :terminalId, :date, :counter, ...)
ON CONFLICT(...) DO UPDATE SET daily_order_counter = MAX(daily_order_counter, :counter)
```

This ensures the counter never goes backwards after a server pull.

**Usage in BillingViewModel:**
```kotlin
val dailyCounter = restaurantRepository.incrementAndGetTerminalDailyCounter(terminalIdentity.terminalId)
val displayId = OrderIdManager.getDailyOrderDisplay(today, dailyCounter, terminalSeries)
```

---

### 10. `terminalSeries` in Bill Creation

**File:** `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\Android\app\src\main\java\com\khanabook\lite\pos\ui\viewmodel\BillingViewModel.kt`

The `terminalSeries` is used in several ways:
1. **Invoice identity** (lines 66-82):
   ```kotlin
   val terminalSeries = sessionManager.getTerminalSeries()
   val displaySeries = terminalSeries.first().uppercaseChar().toString()
   val invoiceSeries = "$financialYear$terminalSeries"
   val sequence = billRepository.getMaxInvoiceSequence(invoiceSeries) + 1L
   val invoiceNumber = "$displaySeries${sequence.toString().padStart(2, '0')}"
   ```
   Example: terminal series `"A"` → display series `"A"`, invoice number `"A01"`.

2. **Daily order display** (via `OrderIdManager.getDailyOrderDisplay`):
   ```kotlin
   val displayId = OrderIdManager.getDailyOrderDisplay(today, dailyCounter, terminalSeries)
   ```

3. **Stored on BillEntity** as `terminalSeries` — used in `getInvoiceNumberDisplay()` for generating fallback invoice numbers.

---

### 11. How the App Handles "No Terminal" / "Pending Approval" States

**No terminal (fresh install, never activated):**
- `sessionManager.isTerminalReady()` returns `false`.
- Every sync cycle calls `ensureTerminalActivated()`.
- `requireActiveTerminalIdentity()` in BillingViewModel (line 84-91) checks `identity == null || !identity.isActive || identity.terminalSeries.isBlank()` and shows an error: `"Terminal is not ready. Sync terminal setup and try again."`.

**Pending approval:**
- `SyncManager.ensureTerminalActivated()` throws `TerminalPendingApprovalException`.
- In `InitialSyncViewModel`, this is caught and the state becomes `PendingApproval(requestId)`.
- The `InitialSyncScreen` shows "Waiting for Approval" with auto-polling every 15 seconds.
- The user stays on this screen until the admin approves/rejects.

**Rejection cooldown (HTTP 429):**
- Throws `TerminalPendingApprovalException(rejectionCooldown=true)`.
- Message: `"Device was recently rejected. Please wait before requesting again."`

**Deactivated by admin (HTTP 403):**
- Throws `IllegalStateException("Terminal has been deactivated by admin. Contact your shop owner.")`.

---

### 12. Device Registration Requests

**Initial request:** Automatic — happens inside `ensureTerminalActivated()` when `isTerminalReady()` is false. Calls `POST /api/v1/sync/terminal/activate` with `{ deviceId, deviceModel }`.

**Request status polling:** Manual/automatic — `GET /api/v1/sync/terminal/request-status/{requestId}`.

**Complete activation:** `POST /api/v1/sync/terminal/complete-activation` with `{ requestId, deviceId }`.

**Tracking:** The `requestId` is embedded in the `TerminalPendingApprovalException` and flows through `InitialSyncState.PendingApproval(requestId)` to the UI. There is no persistent storage of the `requestId` — if the app is killed during the pending state, the next login triggers a fresh activation request (which the server handles by returning either the existing pending request or a new one).

---

### 13. What Happens on Reinstall / New Device (Terminal Recovery)

**Reclaim API exists but is NOT called from Android:**
- `listTerminals()` and `reclaimTerminal()` are defined in `KhanaBookApi` but no Android code calls them. They are available for future use.

**Current behavior on reinstall:**
1. User logs in → gets a new `deviceId` (UUID generated fresh).
2. Initial sync starts → `ensureTerminalActivated()` fires.
3. Since `isTerminalReady()` is false (new device, no terminal identity stored), a new activation request is sent.
4. The server either:
   - Approves automatically (for trusted devices) → new terminal registered.
   - Goes into pending approval → admin must approve.
5. The new terminal gets a new `terminalId` and `terminalSeries`.

**What persists across reinstall:**
- Nothing. `SharedPreferences` are cleared on app data clear. The `deviceId` is regenerated. The user must go through the full activation flow again.

**What the DB migration does for legacy bills:**
- Migration 57→58 adds `terminal_id`, `created_terminal_id`, `created_device_id`, `current_owner_terminal_id` columns.
- Legacy bills are backfilled: `terminal_id` and `created_terminal_id` get `COALESCE(terminal_series, 'LEGACY_UNRESOLVED')`.
- Migration 59→60 adds `record_origin`/`record_scope` columns with conservative defaults:
  - Unsynced bills → `local_created`/`terminal_operational`
  - In-progress drafts → `local_created`/`terminal_operational`
  - Marketplace → `marketplace_imported`/`restaurant_shared`
  - All other synced history → `server_imported`/`restaurant_history`
- The runtime `reconcileLocalBillScope()` (called after every pull) re-labels this terminal's own bills to `local_created`/`terminal_operational`.

---

### Architecture Summary

```
Login (AuthViewModel)
  └─ UserRepository.remoteLogin()
       └─ Saves auth token, restaurantId, role
       └─ Switches to restaurant-specific DB
       └─ Triggers initial sync → MasterSyncWorker

Initial Sync Flow (InitialSyncViewModel / InitialSyncScreen)
  └─ performFullSync() [SyncManager]
       └─ ensureTerminalActivated()
            ├─ POST /terminal/activate → 200: Save TerminalIdentity
            ├─ POST /terminal/activate → 202: PendingApproval → Poll /request-status/{id}
            │    └─ APPROVED → POST /complete-activation → Save TerminalIdentity → retry sync
            │    └─ REJECTED/EXPIRED → Error state
            └─ POST /terminal/activate → 403: Deactivated error

  └─ pushAll() [MasterSyncProcessor]
       └─ Pushes bills with terminalId, createdTerminalId, currentOwnerTerminalId, terminalSeries

  └─ pullAndPersistMasterData() [SyncManager]
       └─ GET /sync/master/pull?terminalId=...
       └─ insertMasterData() → saves bills with terminal ownership fields
       └─ reconcileLocalBillScope() → re-labels this terminal's bills as operational

Bill Creation (BillingViewModel)
  └─ requireActiveTerminalIdentity() → checks isActive + terminalSeries not blank
  └─ restaurantRepository.incrementAndGetTerminalDailyCounter(terminalId)
  └─ BillEntity with terminalId = createdTerminalId = currentOwnerTerminalId = terminalId
  └─ terminalSeries set from sessionManager.getTerminalSeries()

Daily Operations (BillRepository)
  └─ All queries scoped by currentTerminalScope(): terminalId → terminalSeries → "LEGACY_UNRESOLVED"
  └─ All mutations guarded by getOperationalBillById() + isLocallyOwned() defense-in-depth

HTTP Layer (AuthInterceptor)
  └─ Every request gets X-Device-Id + X-Terminal-Token (if available)
```
</task_result>
</task>
```

| 15 | `C:\Users\nandh\Desktop\Khanabook\KhanaBook\server\src\main\java\com\khanabook\saas\controller\TerminalController.java` | **Android sync controller** — activation, reclaim, complete-activation, transfer, request-status (not called from web-admin) |

## 2. API Endpoints Called by Web-Admin (from `business-api.service.ts`)

| Method | HTTP Call | Endpoint | Purpose |
|--------|-----------|----------|---------|
| `getTerminals()` | `GET` | `/business/terminals` | List all registered terminals for the authenticated restaurant |
| `renameTerminal(id, {name})` | `POST` | `/business/terminals/{id}/rename` | Rename a terminal |
| `deactivateTerminal(id)` | `POST` | `/business/terminals/{id}/deactivate` | Deactivate a terminal (marks INACTIVE, revokes tokens) |
| `reactivateTerminal(id)` | `POST` | `/business/terminals/{id}/reactivate` | Reactivate a deactivated terminal (BusinessAdminController) |
| `getTerminalRequests(status)` | `GET` | `/business/terminal-requests?status=ALL` | List device registration requests, filtered by status |
| `approveTerminalRequest(id)` | `POST` | `/business/terminal-requests/{id}/approve` | Approve a pending device request (creates/activates terminal) |
| `rejectTerminalRequest(id, {reason?})` | `POST` | `/business/terminal-requests/{id}/reject` | Reject a pending device request |
| `recoverTerminal(id, {deviceId})` | `POST` | `/business/terminals/{id}/recover` | Recover/rebind terminal to a new device (not used by current UI but exposed in service) |

---

## 3. UI Flow for Terminal Management

### Page Layout (`terminals-page.component.ts`)

The page is a single standalone Angular component with two major sections plus three confirmation dialogs:

#### Section 1: "Registered Terminals" (top)
- **Header** with count badges: `{n} Registered` and `{n} Pending`
- **Refresh** button to reload
- **Data table** with columns: Name, Series, Device, Status, Active, Updated, Action
- **Loading state**: 4 skeleton rows
- **Empty state**: 📟 icon + "No terminals registered yet" message

**Per-terminal actions:**
- **Rename** (any terminal): Click the "Rename" button → inline text input appears with Save/Cancel buttons. Saves via `POST /terminals/{id}/rename`.
- **Deactivate** (active terminals only): Click "Deactivate" → confirm dialog with `confirmDanger=true` → on confirm calls `POST /terminals/{id}/deactivate`. The terminal status is updated locally to `INACTIVE` / `isActive: false`.
- **Reactivate** (inactive terminals, only if `canManageTerminals()`): Click "Reactivate" → confirm dialog → on confirm calls `POST /terminals/{id}/reactivate`. Shows error toast `MAX_ACTIVE_TERMINALS_REACHED` if the 5-terminal limit blocks it.

#### Section 2: "Device Requests" (below terminals section)
- **Header** with filter toggle buttons: "Pending" (default) | "All"
- **Data table** with columns: Device, Model, Type, Status, Requested, Action
- **Empty state**: 🔔 icon + "No device requests" message

**Per-request actions (only for PENDING requests):**
- **Approve**: Click "Approve" → calls `POST /terminal-requests/{id}/approve` → updates local status to `APPROVED`
- **Reject**: Click "Reject" → confirm dialog with `confirmDanger=true` → on confirm calls `POST /terminal-requests/{id}/reject` → updates local status to `REJECTED`
- **Already processed** (non-PENDING): Shows `rejectionReason` or `-`

#### Confirmation Dialogs (3 modals)
1. **Deactivate Terminal**: Shows terminal name, "Deactivate" (danger styled) / "Cancel" buttons
2. **Reactivate Terminal**: Shows terminal name, warns about the 5-active-terminal limit, "Reactivate" / "Cancel" buttons
3. **Reject Device Request**: Shows device name, "Reject" (danger styled) / "Cancel" buttons

---

## 4. Role-Based Access

### Route Protection (`app.routes.ts`)
```
path: 'business/terminals'
roles: ['OWNER', 'SHOP_ADMIN']
```
Both roles can access the page. The role guard (`roleGuard`) checks `session.role` against the allowed list.

### Sidebar Visibility (`sidebar-layout.component.ts`)
- **OWNER**: Full sidebar — Dashboard, Orders, Menu, Staff, **Devices** (all 5 links)
- **SHOP_ADMIN**: Only **Devices** link shown in sidebar (their single-purpose role)
- **KBOOK_ADMIN**: Platform Dashboard and Businesses (no terminal access)

### Post-Login Redirect (`auth.service.ts`)
- **OWNER** → `/business/dashboard`
- **SHOP_ADMIN** → `/business/terminals` (directly lands on the terminal management page)

### UI-Level Permission (`terminals-page.component.ts`, line 403-406)
```typescript
canManageTerminals(): boolean {
  const role = this.auth.session()?.role;
  return role === 'OWNER' || role === 'SHOP_ADMIN';
}
```
This method controls:
- Whether the **Reactivate** button is shown for inactive terminals
- For SHOP_ADMIN without manage permission: inactive terminals show a muted "Deactivated" label instead of the Reactivate button

**Important distinction**: Both roles can technically manage terminals (the `canManageTerminals()` check always returns true for both). But the **Reactivate** button is specifically gated by `canManageTerminals()` — so if a future change restricts this, SHOP_ADMIN would lose reactivate ability. Currently both roles have full management capability.

### Server-side Endpoint Security
- **`/business/terminals/**` and `/business/terminal-requests/**`**: Secured via `SecurityConfig` for authenticated business users (OWNER/SHOP_ADMIN). The `TerminalManagementController` does NOT have `@RequireRole` annotations — it relies on the broader security context.
- **`/business/terminals/{id}/reactivate`**: Uses `@RequireRole({UserRole.OWNER, UserRole.SHOP_ADMIN})` — explicitly allows both.
- **Staff management / Menu management**: Use `@RequireRole(UserRole.OWNER)` only — SHOP_ADMIN cannot manage these.

---

## 5. Server-Side Terminal Lifecycle (Business Logic)

### `TerminalManagementService` — Core Rules

| Operation | Key Logic |
|-----------|-----------|
| **Approval** (`approveRequest`) | Locks restaurant profile (pessimistic). For RECOVERY type: rebinds existing terminal, checks 5-term limit if transitioning from non-ACTIVE. For NEW_DEVICE: allocates next available series (A, B, C... Z, T27, T28...), assigns terminal name "Terminal {series}", checks 5-active limit. Increments `credentialVersion` on recovery (revokes old tokens). |
| **Rejection** (`rejectRequest`) | Marks request as REJECTED with optional `rejectionReason`. Sets `processedAt`. Does NOT affect any terminal. |
| **Deactivation** (`deactivateTerminal`) | Sets `status=INACTIVE`, `isActive=false`. Increments `credentialVersion` (revokes all existing terminal tokens for that terminal). |
| **Reactivate** (`BusinessWriteService.reactivateTerminal`) | Lock restaurant profile. Only works on INACTIVE terminals. Checks 5-active limit. Sets `status=ACTIVE`, `isActive=true`. Increments `credentialVersion`. |
| **Rename** (`renameTerminal`) | Updates `terminalName` only. No state changes. |
| **Recovery** (`recoverTerminal`) | Lock restaurant. Validates eligibility via `validateRecoveryEligibility()`. If transitioning from non-ACTIVE → ACTIVE, checks 5-term limit. Binds new deviceId. Increments `credentialVersion`. Generates new terminal token. |
| **Series Allocation** (`allocateNextSeries`) | Scans existing terminals, finds first unused letter (A-Z) or numbers T27+. |

### 5-Active-Terminal Limit
Enforced atomically in:
- `approveRequest()` — before creating a new terminal or reactivating a recovered one
- `recoverTerminal()` — when transitioning from non-ACTIVE to ACTIVE
- `BusinessWriteService.reactivateTerminal()` — when reactivating from INACTIVE
- Uses `restaurantProfileRepository.findAndLockByRestaurantId()` for pessimistic locking
- Error code: `TERMINAL_LIMIT_REACHED` (server) / `MAX_ACTIVE_TERMINALS_REACHED` (web-admin UI)

### `DeviceRegistrationRequest` Entity
- **Types**: `NEW_DEVICE` (unknown device), `RECOVERY` (existing terminal reinstall), `REPLACEMENT` (device swap)
- **Deduplication**: At most one PENDING request per device+restaurant (unique partial index)
- **Rejection cooldown**: 5-minute wait after rejection before a new request can be created
- **Statuses**: PENDING → APPROVED / REJECTED / EXPIRED

---

## 6. Summary of Terminal Features Implemented

| Feature | Implemented? | Where |
|---------|-------------|-------|
| List registered terminals | Yes | TerminalManagementController + terminals-page.component |
| Rename terminal | Yes | Inline editing in table, POST to server |
| Deactivate terminal | Yes | Confirm dialog → POST → revoke tokens |
| Reactivate terminal | Yes | Confirm dialog → POST → 5-limit check |
| Approve device request | Yes | Table button → POST → creates/recovers terminal |
| Reject device request | Yes | Confirm dialog → POST → marks rejected |
| Filter requests (Pending/All) | Yes | UI toggle buttons, server query param `status=ALL` |
| 5-terminal limit enforcement | Yes | Atomic lock + counter check on approval/recovery/reactivate |
| Terminal series auto-allocation | Yes | A, B, C... Z, T27+ |
| Credential versioning / token revocation | Yes | Incremented on deactivate, recovery, reactivate |
| Rejection cooldown (5 min) | Yes | Server-side, returns null from `createOrReuseRegistrationRequest` |
| Recovery/rebind terminal to new device | Yes (API ready) | `POST /recover` endpoint exists, not exposed in current UI |
| Self-service reclaim after reinstall | No (Android only) | `POST /sync/terminal/reclaim` via TerminalController |
| Device request polling from Android | No (Android only) | `GET /sync/terminal/request-status/{id}` via TerminalController |
| Completion of activation from Android | No (Android only) | `POST /sync/terminal/complete-activation` via TerminalController |
| Bill transfer between terminals | No (Android only) | `POST /sync/terminal/transfer` via TerminalController |
| Role distinction (OWNER vs SHOP_ADMIN) | Partial | SHOP_ADMIN can only see Devices page; both can fully manage terminals; OWNER has additional access to dashboard, orders, menu, staff |
</task_result>
</task>
```

# KhanaBook Terminal Sets — Deep Analysis

## 1. Terminal Lifecycle (End-to-End)

### State Machine

```
                    ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
                    │                                                 │
                    v                                                 │
  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  approve  ┌──────────┐  deactivate  ┌──────────┐
  │ UNKNOWN  │→ │ PENDING  │ ────────→ │ ACTIVE   │ ────────────→│ INACTIVE │
  │ (device) │  │ (request)│           │ (terminal)│              │          │
  └──────────┘  └──────────┘           └──────────┘              └──────────┘
                     │                      │  reactivate             │
                     │ reject               │ ←───────────────────────┘
                     v                      │
                ┌──────────┐                │
                │ REJECTED │                │
                └──────────┘                │
                     │                      │ recover (rebind device)
                     v                      │
                (5-min cooldown)            │
                                           v
                                      ┌──────────┐
                                      │ ACTIVE   │
                                      │ (new dev)│
                                      └──────────┘
```

### Activation Paths (4 ways a terminal goes ACTIVE)

| Path | Trigger | Who | Credential rotation? |
|---|---|---|---|
| **First-ever** | OWNER activates unowning device | Android `POST /sync/terminal/activate` | N/A (fresh) |
| **Re-auth** | Known device with valid token | Android `POST /sync/terminal/activate` | No (heartbeat only) |
| **Admin approve** | PENDING request approved | Web-admin `POST /terminal-requests/{id}/approve` | Yes (recovery) or No (new) |
| **Admin reactivate** | INACTIVE terminal reactivated | Web-admin `POST /terminals/{id}/reactivate` | Yes (+1) |

### Files Involved (by layer)

**Server:**
- `TerminalController.java` — Android-facing endpoints (activate, reclaim, complete-activation, transfer)
- `TerminalManagementController.java` — Web-admin endpoints (list, deactivate, rename, requests, approve, reject, recover)
- `BusinessAdminController.java` — Reactivate endpoint
- `TerminalManagementService.java` — Core logic (approve, reject, deactivate, recover, rename, series allocation, 5-limit)
- `BusinessWriteService.java` — `reactivateTerminal()` with limit check
- `TerminalRequestFilter.java` — Validates `X-Terminal-Token` on every request (credential version, status check)
- `JwtUtility.java` — `generateTerminalToken()` with `credVer` claim
- `SecurityAuditService.java` — Logs every terminal lifecycle event

**Android:**
- `SyncManager.kt:68-150` — `ensureTerminalActivated()` called at every sync cycle
- `SessionManager.kt` — Persists `terminal_id`, `terminal_series`, `terminal_token` in SharedPreferences
- `InitialSyncViewModel.kt` + `InitialSyncScreen.kt` — Two-phase activation UI (poll → complete)
- `AuthInterceptor.kt` — Sends `X-Terminal-Token` on every API request
- `BillingViewModel.kt` — `requireActiveTerminalIdentity()` gates bill creation

**Web-admin:**
- `terminals-page.component.ts` — Full management UI: list, rename, deactivate, reactivate, approve, reject
- `business-api.service.ts` — All terminal API calls

---

## 2. Terminal Ownership Model

### Bill-Level Ownership Fields

| Column | Set at creation | Mutable? | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|
| `created_terminal_id` | Terminal's ID | Never | Bill's origin terminal (forever) |
| `current_owner_terminal_id` | Terminal's ID | Via `/sync/terminal/transfer` | Current operational owner |
| `created_device_id` | Device UUID | Never | Physical device that created it |
| `terminal_id` | Terminal's ID | Yes (overwritten by server on push) | Last-modified terminal |
| `terminal_series` | e.g., "A" | No | Human-readable series |

### How Android Sets Ownership

Every bill creation in `BillingViewModel`:

```kotlin
BillEntity(
    terminalId = terminalIdentity.terminalId,
    createdTerminalId = terminalIdentity.terminalId,
    createdDeviceId = terminalIdentity.deviceId,
    currentOwnerTerminalId = terminalIdentity.terminalId,
    terminalSeries = sessionManager.getTerminalSeries(),
    ...
)
```

### How Server Enforces Ownership

**`BillTerminalUtil.java`** — the authorization gate for all bill mutations:

1. **isFinalized(bill):** `orderStatus` = completed/paid/cancelled, OR `refundAmount > 0`, OR marketplace source → immutable
2. **isModifiableByTerminal(bill, terminalId, deviceId, isAdmin):**
   - Finalized → block (unless admin or owning terminal)
   - Admin → always allow
   - No owner → allow (pre-terminal legacy)
   - `LEGACY_UNRESOLVED` → only original device (by `createdDeviceId`)
   - No `trustedTerminalId` → allow (strict mode disabled)
   - Otherwise → must match `currentOwnerTerminalId` exactly

**`GenericSyncService.java`** — on every push:
- Overwrites client-sent terminal fields with trusted terminal context
- Rejects cross-terminal child record attachments
- Rejects pushes to another terminal's finalized bills

### Android Local Query Scoping

`BillRepository.currentTerminalScope()`:
```kotlin
sessionManager.getTerminalId()          // UUID like "term_a1b2c3"
    ?: sessionManager.getTerminalSeries() // fallback "A"
    ?: "LEGACY_UNRESOLVED"                // last resort
```

Every query passes through `getOperationalBillById()` which now filters by `currentOwnerTerminalId` + marketplace exclusion (no longer by fragile `recordOrigin`/`recordScope`).

---

## 3. Multi-Device Invoice Numbering

### Invoice Number Format

```
{financial_year}{terminal_series}{sequence}
     e.g.,  26         A             08       → "26A08"
```

### How It's Allocated

**Server-side (production path):**
1. `BillServiceImpl.allocateMissingInvoiceNumbers()` runs on every push
2. Locks the terminal row via `findAndLockByRestaurantIdAndTerminalSeries()` (pessimistic write lock)
3. Reads current max sequence for that `(restaurant_id, financial_year, invoice_series)`
4. Assigns next sequence + generates invoice number
5. If `findAndLock` returns null (terminal doesn't exist) → skips allocation (bill still succeeds without invoice)

**Android-side (fallback for offline):**
1. `BillingViewModel` reads `sessionManager.getTerminalSeries()` → e.g., "A"
2. Reads `maxInvoiceSequence` from local DB
3. Generates: `invoiceNumber = "A" + (sequence).toString().padStart(2, '0')`
4. Server may overwrite this on push with the authoritative server-allocated number

### Database Uniqueness

```sql
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX ux_bills_restaurant_invoice_series_active
    ON bills (restaurant_id, financial_year, invoice_series, invoice_sequence)
    WHERE is_deleted = false AND invoice_number IS NOT NULL;
```

Also `ux_bills_restaurant_terminal_daily_active` for per-terminal daily order numbers:
```sql
ON bills (restaurant_id, last_reset_date, terminal_series, daily_order_id)
WHERE is_deleted = false;
```

### Terminal Series Allocation Algorithm

```java
private String allocateNextSeries(Long restaurantId) {
    // Scans A..Z, then T27, T28, ...
    int n = 1;
    while (true) {
        String candidate = n <= 26
            ? String.valueOf((char) ('A' + n - 1))
            : "T" + n;
        if (!assigned.contains(candidate)) return candidate;
        n++;
    }
}
```

First terminal always gets `"A"` (hardcoded in `TerminalController.activate()`).

---

## 4. Device Registration Request Flow

### State Machine

```
PENDING ──approve──→ APPROVED ──complete-activation──→ (device gets token)
   │                                                     │
   └──reject──→ REJECTED ──(5-min cooldown)──→ can retry
   │
   └──timeout──→ EXPIRED (not implemented)
```

### Three Request Types

| Type | When | Server behavior on approve |
|---|---|---|
| `NEW_DEVICE` | Unknown device registers | Creates new `RestaurantTerminal`, allocates series, creates token |
| `RECOVERY` | Known device reinstalls (deviceId matched) | Reuses existing terminal, rebinds deviceId, rotates credential |
| `REPLACEMENT` | Admin replaces physical device | Same as recovery (admin-initiated rebind) |

### API Flow (Android → Server → Web-admin)

```
Android                        Server                       Web-admin
  │                              │                             │
  ├─ POST /terminal/activate ───→│                             │
  │   {deviceId, deviceModel}    │                             │
  │                              ├─ No terminal found          │
  │                              ├─ Creates PENDING request    │
  │←─ 202 {requestId, message}   │                             │
  │                              │                             │
  │  ── poll loop ──             │                             │
  │  GET /request-status/{id} ──→│                             │
  │←─ {status: "PENDING"}        │                             │
  │                              │           ┌─────────────────┤
  │                              │           │ POST /approve   │
  │                              │           │←────────────────┤
  │                              ├─ Creates terminal           │
  │                              ├─ Status → APPROVED          │
  │                              │           ├────────────────→│
  │  GET /request-status/{id} ──→│                             │
  │←─ {status: "APPROVED"}       │                             │
  │                              │                             │
  ├─ POST /complete-activation ─→│                             │
  │   {requestId, deviceId}      │                             │
  │←─ {terminalToken, series...} │                             │
  │                              │                             │
  └─ Saves TerminalIdentity      │                             │
```

### Important Security Properties

- **Request status API** never returns credentials — only `APPROVED`/`REJECTED`/`PENDING`
- **Complete activation** validates deviceId matches the request → proves same installation
- **Credential version** increments on every lifecycle change → old tokens instantly invalid
- **Rejection cooldown** (5 min) prevents spam re-requests
- **Pessimistic locking** on approval/rejection → no race conditions on terminal creation

---

## 5. Sync Scoping (What Each Terminal Sees)

### Push (Android → Server)

Terminal pushes ALL its records. Server enforces:
- Terminal fields are overwritten from the trusted `X-Terminal-Token` context (client cannot fake ownership)
- Cross-terminal pushes to another terminal's finalized bills are rejected
- `GenericSyncService.strictMode`: rejects pushes without terminal token (configurable via `terminal.sync.strict`)

### Pull (Server → Android)

Master pull filters bills by terminal:
```sql
WHERE created_terminal_id = :terminalId
   OR current_owner_terminal_id = :terminalId
```

This means:
- Terminal A sees bills it created AND bills transferred to it
- Terminal A does NOT see Terminal B's bills (unless transferred)
- All non-bill data (menu, categories, profiles, users) is unfiltered — shared across all terminals

### Post-Pull Reconciliation (Android)

`MasterSyncProcessor.reconcileLocalBillScope()` re-labels pulled bills:
- Bills where `createdTerminalId == thisTerminal` → `local_created`/`terminal_operational`
- Marketplace bills → `marketplace_imported`/`restaurant_shared`
- Everything else → `server_imported`/`restaurant_history`

### Terminal Daily Counter

Per-terminal, per-day order number sequencing via `terminal_daily_counter` table:
```sql
PRIMARY KEY (restaurant_id, terminal_id, date)
```
Seeded after every pull from the max existing local daily order. Prevents duplicate order numbers after reinstall.

---

## 6. Token & Security Model

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      X-Terminal-Token                        │
│  JWT Claims: { tokenType: "terminal",                       │
│                terminalId, terminalSeries, deviceId,         │
│                credVer, restaurantId, role }                 │
│  Lifetime: 30 days (configurable)                           │
└─────────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘
                          │
                          v
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  TerminalRequestFilter (runs on every request)              │
│  1. Validate token type = "terminal"                        │
│  2. Cross-check restaurantId matches auth JWT               │
│  3. Look up terminal in DB                                  │
│  4. credVer must match DB credential_version exactly        │
│  5. Status must be ACTIVE                                   │
│  6. Set TenantContext for downstream code                   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Credential Version Lifecycle

| Operation | `credential_version` change | Effect |
|---|---|---|
| Terminal created | Set to 1 | First token issued |
| Deactivated | +1 | All existing tokens revoked |
| Reactivated | +1 | Must issue new token |
| Recovered (rebind device) | +1 | Old tokens invalid |
| Reclaimed (post-reinstall) | +1 | Old tokens invalid |
| Approved (RECOVERY type) | +1 | Old tokens invalid |

Any token with `credVer < DB` is rejected → forces re-authentication.

---

## 7. Found Gaps & Risks

| # | Issue | Impact | Layer |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | `device_registration_request` has **no FK constraints** to `users`, `restaurantprofiles`, or `restaurant_terminal` | Orphaned requests, phantom user/terminal references | DB |
| 2 | `RestaurantTerminal` entity has no `@OneToMany` or `@ManyToOne` to `DeviceRegistrationRequest` | No cascade, no integrity | JPA |
| 3 | No `ON DELETE RESTRICT` on `restaurant_terminal` rows that have bills referencing `terminal_series` | Deleting a terminal orphans its bills' `terminal_series` reference | DB |
| 4 | `Android: reclaimTerminal()` defined in `KhanaBookApi` but **never called** from Android code | No self-service post-reinstall recovery; device always goes through PENDING approval | Android |
| 5 | `terminal.sync.strict` and `terminal.sync.compatibility` are config properties — if disabled, tokens become optional | Without strict mode, non-terminal clients could push data | Server |
| 6 | `LEGACY_UNRESOLVED` sentinel value on `currentOwnerTerminalId`/`createdTerminalId` | Ambiguous — cannot distinguish pre-migration from actual errors | DB |
| 7 | Web-admin `recoverTerminal()` endpoint exists but **no UI button** calls it | Admin must use approve flow instead of direct recovery | Web-admin |
| 8 | Invoice numbers generated offline on Android may conflict with server-allocated numbers on push | Potential duplicate or gap in sequence if server re-allocates | Android |

---

## 8. Summary: Terminal Sets Architecture

```
                    ┌──────────────────────┐
                    │   restaurant_terminal │  (server-owned registry)
                    │   ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐    │
                    │   │  A  │ │  B  │ ... │  ≤5 active terminals per restaurant
                    │   └─────┘ └─────┘    │
                    └──────────┬───────────┘
                               │
            ┌──────────────────┼──────────────────┐
            │                  │                  │
            v                  v                  v
     ┌──────────┐      ┌──────────┐      ┌──────────┐
     │ Terminal │      │ Terminal │      │ Terminal │
     │    A     │      │    B     │      │    C     │
     ├──────────┤      ├──────────┤      ├──────────┤
     │ Series A │      │ Series B │      │ Series C │
     │ Token v1 │      │ Token v1 │      │ Token v3 │
     │ Daily# 1 │      │ Daily# 1 │      │ Daily# 5 │
     │ Inv# A01 │      │ Inv# B01 │      │ Inv# C05 │
     └──────────┘      └──────────┘      └──────────┘
          │                  │                  │
          │      ┌───────────┼───────────┐      │
          │      │           │           │      │
          v      v           v           v      v
     ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐
     │              Bills (restaurant)           │
     │  A: created_terminal_id=A, owner=A       │
     │  B: created_terminal_id=B, owner=B       │
     │  C: created_terminal_id=A, owner=C       │ ← transferred
     │  D: created_terminal_id=LEGACY, owner=X  │ ← pre-migration
     └──────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

Each terminal has:
- **Independent invoice series** (`A01`, `B01`, ...)
- **Independent daily order counter** (per `terminal_series` + `last_reset_date`)
- **Independent token** with credential version
- **Own bill set** (bills it created or were transferred to it)
- **Shared everything else** (menu, categories, profiles, users)

Want me to take action on any of the gaps (add FKs, add UI for recover, fix invoice sync collision)?

# KhanaBook V1 — Complete Project Architecture

## 1. Overview

**KhanaBook** is a B2B2C SaaS platform for Indian restaurants. It provides a modern POS system that works offline-first across **Android POS terminals**, a **Spring Boot backend**, and a **web admin dashboard**.

### Business Model
- **B2B:** Restaurants subscribe to the platform
- **B2C:** End customers receive digital invoices, pay via UPI/Easebuzz, order via storefront

### Key Metrics
| Property | Value |
|---|---|
| Codebase age | Production (V1) |
| Active layers | 3 (Android + Server + Web-Admin) |
| Database | PostgreSQL 16 (server) + SQLCipher-encrypted Room/SQLite (Android) |
| Sync model | Offline-first, device → server push + pull |
| Auth | Google Sign-In + Phone OTP + JWT + Terminal Tokens |

## 3. Feature → Implementation Map

### 3.1 Offline-First POS

| Feature | Android | Server | DB |
|---|---|---|---|
| Create bill offline | `BillingViewModel` writes to Room | N/A | `bills` with `is_synced=false`, `local_id` |
| Add items offline | `bill_items` written locally | N/A | `bill_items` with FK to local bill |
| Push when online | `MasterSyncProcessor.pushAll()` | `GenericSyncService` receives + persists | `is_synced=true`, `server_id` assigned |
| Pull to other devices | `MasterSyncProcessor.pullAndPersistMasterData()` | `MasterSyncController.pull()` filters by terminal | `server_updated_at` for delta |
| Conflict resolution | Server-wins with `updatedAt` comparison | `GenericSyncService` overwrites | `version` for optimistic locking |

**Sync protocol:**
- **Push:** DTO → `POST /sync/master/push` → server applies → returns success/failure
- **Pull:** `GET /sync/master/pull?since={timestamp}` → server returns delta → Android upserts via `insertSyncedBills()`
- **Batch:** Items grouped by type (bills, items, payments), processed atomically per batch
- **Transaction safety:** Server-side `SyncTransaction` prevents partial commits; Android `NonCancellable` coroutine prevents mid-air cancellation

### 3.2 UPI QR Payments

| Step | Implementation |
|---|---|
| Collect UPI ID | `restaurantprofiles.upi_handle`, `upi_mobile` — stored server-side (V1) |
| Generate QR | Android: creates QR from `upi://pay?pa={upiId}&am={amount}&pn=KhanaBook` |
| Customer scans | Any UPI app — amount is locked in QR |
| Confirm payment | Bill payment mode set to `upi`, `verified_by='manual'` |
| UPI QR URL (CDN) | `restaurantprofiles.upi_qr_url` + `upi_qr_version` (V18) — for web/storefront |

### 3.3 Invoice Sharing

| Method | Implementation |
|---|---|
| SMS (normal text) | `customer_whatsapp` field, Android sends via `SmsManager` |
| WhatsApp link | Android opens `https://wa.me/{phone}?text={invoiceUrl}` |
| Invoice URL | `public_token` (UUID, V19) → `https://kbook.iadv.cloud/invoice/{token}` |
| Print (customer) | `restaurantprofiles.printer_name`, `printer_mac` |
| Print (kitchen) | `restaurantprofiles.kitchen_printer_name`, `kitchen_printer_mac` (V2) |
| Auto-print on success | `restaurantprofiles.auto_print_on_success` |
| KOT tracking | `KitchenPrintQueueManager` + `kitchen_print_queue` Room table (Android-only) |

### 3.4 Google ML Kit Menu Extraction

| Step | Implementation |
|---|---|
| Capture photo | Android camera intent → `InputImage` from `media.Image` |
| OCR (online/offline) | ML Kit `TextRecognition.getClient()` — works offline |
| Parse structured data | `TextGraphParser` extracts categories, items, prices, variants |
| Manual review | `MenuExtractionScreen` — user corrects before saving |
| Save | Written to `categories` + `menuitems` + `itemvariants` |
| Server backup | Synced via normal push; `menu_extraction_jobs` stores raw extraction |

### 3.5 Multi-Terminal Support

Covered in depth in the Terminal Sets analysis above. Key highlights:
- 5-terminal limit per restaurant
- Per-terminal invoice series (A, B, C...)
- Per-terminal daily order counters
- Per-terminal credential tokens with version-based revocation
- Device registration + admin approval flow
- Bill ownership tracking (`created_terminal_id`, `current_owner_terminal_id`)
- Terminal transfer API (`POST /sync/terminal/transfer`)

### 3.6 Pay-Before-Food vs Pay-After-Food

| Mode | `order_payment_flow_mode` (V24) | Sync behavior |
|---|---|---|
| Pay-after | `pay_after_food` | Bill drafted → items added → finalized. **Two sync cycles** (draft push → update push) |
| Pay-before | `pay_before_food` | Customer pays first → bill created complete. **One sync cycle** |

Server-side: GenericSyncService allows updating bills in multiple sync cycles for draft→complete workflows.

### 3.7 Server-Owned Payments (Easebuzz Gateway)

| Component | Tables | Flow |
|---|---|---|
| Gateway config | `restaurant_payment_config` (V7) — encrypted salt, merchant key | Server-stored, never on device |
| Payment creation | `payments` (V7) | Server creates on checkout |
| Webhook receiver | `easebuzz_webhook_events` (V6) | Raw webhook logged |
| Webhook audit | `payment_webhook_logs` (V7) | Signature validation tracked |
| Refund tracking | `payments.refund_*` columns (V14, V17) | Mode, status, amount, gateway IDs |
| Payment mode distinction | `bill_payments.payment_mode='easebuzz'` (V15, V16) | Distinct from offline `upi` |

Flow: Customer pays via Easebuzz → webhook received → `payments` updated → `bill_payments` updated (via `verified_by='easebuzz'`) → synced to Android on next pull.

### 3.8 Marketplace Orders (Zomato/Swiggy)

| Component | Tables | Flow |
|---|---|---|
| Marketplace orders | `marketplace_orders` (V21) | Received via webhook |
| Order items | `marketplace_order_items` (V21) | Line items from platform |
| Bill linking | `marketplace_orders.bill_id → bills(id)` | Linked to POS bill after acceptance |
| Channel tracking | `bills.source_channel` (V25) = `'zomato'`/`'swiggy'`/`'own_website'` | Persisted for reports |
| Restaurant config | `zomato_outlet_id`, `swiggy_store_id`, API keys, webhook secrets (V20, V21) | On `restaurantprofiles` |

### 3.9 Storefront (Customer Self-Service)

| Component | Tables | Flow |
|---|---|---|
| Customer orders | `customer_orders` (V8) | Placed via web storefront |
| Order items | `customer_order_items` (V8) | Line items |
| Tracking | `public_order_code`, `tracking_token` (V8) | Unique per order |
| Fulfillment | `fulfillment_type` = `'pickup'`/`'delivery'` | Restaurant processes and marks ready |

---

## 4. Data Flow: End-to-End Bill Lifecycle

```
CUSTOMER DINES → BILL CREATED → PAID → SYNCED → REPORTED

┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 1. CREATE (Android, offline)                                      │
│    BillingViewModel.createDraftOnlineBill()                       │
│    ├─ requireActiveTerminalIdentity()                             │
│    ├─ restaurantRepository.incrementAndGetTerminalDailyCounter()  │
│    ├─ Build BillEntity with ownership fields + terminal_series    │
│    ├─ Insert via BillDao (is_synced=false)                        │
│    └─ If KOT printer configured → PrintRouter dispatches KOT      │
│                                                                   │
│ 2. MODIFY (Android, offline)                                      │
│    Add items → BillItemDao inserts (is_synced=false)              │
│    Update payment mode → BillDao.updatePaymentMode()              │
│    Update order status → BillDao.updateOrderStatus()              │
│    All gated by getOperationalBillById() + isLocallyOwned()       │
│                                                                   │
│ 3. PUSH (when online)                                             │
│    WorkManager triggers MasterSyncWorker                          │
│    ├─ performFullSync() [SyncManager]                             │
│    │  ├─ ensureTerminalActivated()                                │
│    │  ├─ pushAll() [MasterSyncProcessor]                          │
│    │  │  ├─ Push bills → POST /sync/master/push                  │
│    │  │  │  Server: GenericSyncService applies + allocates        │
│    │  │  │  invoice number via BillServiceImpl                    │
│    │  │  ├─ Push bill_items                                       │
│    │  │  └─ Push bill_payments                                   │
│    │  └─ pullAndPersistMasterData()                               │
│    │     ├─ GET /sync/master/pull?since={ts}                      │
│    │     ├─ insertMasterData() → upsert into Room                 │
│    │     └─ reconcileLocalBillScope()                             │
│    └─ Update is_synced=true locally                                │
│                                                                   │
│ 4. REPORT (Web-admin or Android Reports tab)                      │
│    ├─ Android ReportsViewModel → BillDao queries (local)          │
│    └─ Web-admin → BusinessAdminController → BillRepository        │
│       Filters: restaurant_id, date range, terminal, status        │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

## 5. Database Schema Summary

### 23 Tables across 42 Flyway migrations

#### Sync Core (12 tables — synced to Android via offline protocol)

| Table | Purpose | Identity Key |
|---|---|---|
| `users` | Auth & staff | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `restaurantprofiles` | Restaurant config | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `categories` | Menu categories | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `menuitems` | Menu items | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `itemvariants` | Item sizes/variants | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `bills` | POS transactions | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `bill_items` | Line items | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `bill_payments` | Payment splits | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `stock_logs` | Inventory movements | `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` |
| `menu_extraction_jobs` | ML Kit OCR results | Server-only |
| `otp_requests` | Phone OTP | Server-only |
| `token_blocklist` | JWT revocation | Server-only |

#### Server-Owned (8 tables — NOT synced to Android)

| Table | Created | Purpose |
|---|---|---|
| `payments` | V7 | Server-side payment records |
| `restaurant_payment_config` | V7 | Encrypted gateway credentials |
| `payment_webhook_logs` | V7 | Webhook audit trail |
| `easebuzz_webhook_events` | V6 | Raw Easebuzz callbacks |
| `customer_orders` | V8 | Storefront orders |
| `customer_order_items` | V8 | Storefront line items |
| `marketplace_orders` | V21 | Zomato/Swiggy orders |
| `marketplace_order_items` | V21 | Marketplace line items |

#### Infrastructure (3 tables — server-managed)

| Table | Created | Purpose |
|---|---|---|
| `restaurant_terminal` | V26 | Terminal registry |
| `device_registration_request` | V41 | Device activation requests |
| `security_audit_log` | V29 | Audit trail |

#### Key Schema Patterns

- **Tenant isolation:** `restaurant_id` on every sync table + composite FKs `(restaurant_id, id)` since V3
- **Offline identity:** `(restaurant_id, device_id, local_id)` UNIQUE on every sync table
- **Sync tracking:** `server_updated_at`, `is_deleted`, `version` for delta pull + soft delete
- **Terminal ownership:** `created_terminal_id`, `current_owner_terminal_id`, `terminal_id`, `terminal_series` on bills (V26, V28, V40)

## 6. Security Model

### Authentication Layers

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 1. Google Sign-In / Phone OTP            │
│    → JWT (auth_token)                    │
│    Claims: userId, restaurantId, role    │
│    Validated by JwtRequestFilter         │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 2. Terminal Token                        │
│    → Signed JWT (terminal_token)         │
│    Claims: terminalId, series, deviceId, │
│             credVer, restaurantId        │
│    Validated by TerminalRequestFilter    │
│    Revocable via credential_version      │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 3. API Security                          │
│    Spring Security filter chain:         │
│    JwtRequestFilter → TerminalFilter →   │
│    SecurityConfig path rules             │
│    Admin IP allowlist for KBOOK_ADMIN    │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### Authorization Matrix

| Scope | KBOOK_ADMIN | OWNER | SHOP_ADMIN |
|---|---|---|---|
| Platform admin (`/admin/**`) | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Business management (`/business/**`) | ❌ | ✅ | ❌ |
| Terminal management | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ |
| Sync (`/sync/**`) | ✅ (read) | ✅ | ✅ (terminal only) |
| Actuator (`/actuator/**`) | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Bill modification (others' bills) | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Terminal transfer | ❌ | ✅ | ✅ |
| Staff management | ❌ | ✅ | ❌ |

### Data Security

- **SQLCipher** on Android Room DB — encrypted at rest
- **Encrypted salt** in `restaurant_payment_config` — AES-GCM, Base64, minimum 32 chars
- **Terminal token credential version** — immediate revocation on deactivation/recovery
- **Security audit log** — all terminal lifecycle events, bill modifications, auth events

---

## 7. Offline Sync Architecture (Detailed)

### Push Protocol

```
Android                              Server
  │                                    │
  ├─ POST /sync/master/push ──────────→│
  │   { bills: [...],                  │
  │     billItems: [...],              │
  │     billPayments: [...],           │
  │     categories: [...],             │
  │     menuItems: [...],              │
  │     itemVariants: [...],           │
  │     stockLogs: [...],              │
  │     users: [...],                  │
  │     profiles: [...],              │
  │     operationId: "uuid" }          │
  │                                    │
  │                          GenericSyncService:
  │                          ├─ Validate tenant + terminal ownership
  │                          ├─ Upsert each record
  │                          ├─ Allocate invoice numbers
  │                          ├─ Backfill server IDs to child records
  │                          └─ Commit SyncTransaction
  │                                    │
  │←─ 200 { success, failedLocalIds }  │
  │                                    │
  └─ Mark is_synced=true for success   │
```

### Pull Protocol

```
Android                              Server
  │                                    │
  ├─ GET /sync/master/pull ───────────→│
  │   ?since={timestamp}               │
  │   &terminalId={terminalId}         │
  │   (X-Terminal-Token in header)     │
  │                                    │
  │                          MasterSyncController:
  │                          ├─ Resolve terminal identity from token
  │                          ├─ Query all entities since timestamp
  │                          ├─ Filter bills by terminal ownership
  │                          └─ Return MasterSyncResponse
  │                                    │
  │←─ 200 { bills: [...],             │
  │         billItems: [...],          │
  │         ...                        │
  │         serverTimestamp }          │
  │                                    │
  ├─ insertMasterData()                │
  │  ├─ Upsert bills via               │
  │  │  insertSyncedBills()            │
  │  ├─ Upsert items + payments        │
  │  └─ Commit Room transaction        │
  ├─ reconcileLocalBillScope()         │
  └─ saveLastSyncTimestamp()           │
```

### Key Design Decisions

| Decision | Rationale |
|---|---|
| Server-wins on conflict | Simpler than CRDT; `updatedAt` comparison |
| Full push every cycle | Android pushes only unsynced rows (`is_synced=false`) |
| Delta pull | Server returns only rows where `server_updated_at > since` |
| Transaction-safe push | Server uses `SyncTransaction` table; failure means retry |
| NonCancellable sync | Android prevents mid-sync cancellation (screen rotate, app background) |
| Follow-up sync loop | If new data was created during sync, queue another cycle |

---

## 8. Deployment

### Production Infrastructure

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                 Hostinger VPS                         │
│                                                      │
│  Apache (reverse proxy)                              │
│  ├─ /api/v1/* → 127.0.0.1:8081 (Spring Boot)        │
│  ├─ / → /var/www/kbook.iadv.cloud/web (Angular SPA) │
│  └─ SSL via Let's Encrypt                            │
│                                                      │
│  Docker Compose stack:                               │
│  ├─ postgres:16 (port 5432)                         │
│  └─ server (Spring Boot JAR, port 8081)             │
│                                                      │
│  CDN: cdn.kbook.iadv.cloud                           │
│  └─ /restaurants/{id}/logo.png, /upi_qr.png         │
│                                                      │
│  Monitoring: /actuator/health (open endpoint)        │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### CI/CD Flow

```
Local dev → git push → GitHub → VPS git pull → deploy-production.sh
                                                         │
                    ┌────────────────────────────────────┤
                    v                                    v
           deploy-production.sh                deploy-web.sh
           (Docker build + up -d)              (npm ci + ng build + rsync)
```

### Database Safety

- **Flyway migrations** — versioned, idempotent, validated against `flyway_schema_history`
- **Backup before deploy** — `ops/backup_postgres.sh` for rollback safety
- **Rollback** — `ops/restore_postgres.sh <backup.sql.gz>` if migration breaks

---

## 9. Known Integrity Gaps (P0-P1)

| Priority | Issue | File/Migration | Fix |
|---|---|---|---|
| **P0** | `payments.bill_id` has no FK constraint | V7 | Add `FOREIGN KEY (restaurant_id, bill_id) REFERENCES bills(restaurant_id, id)` |
| **P0** | `device_registration_request` has zero FKs | V41 | Add FKs to restaurantprofiles, users, restaurant_terminal |
| **P1** | `bill.cancel_reason` — entity has TEXT, V1 has VARCHAR(500) | `Bill.java` / V1 | Align entity to `@Column(length=500)` |
| **P1** | `source_channel` blank for POS bills | V25 backfill | Update: `SET source_channel = 'POS' WHERE blank AND not marketplace` |
| **P1** | Android `reclaimTerminal()` API defined but never called | `KhanaBookApi.kt` | Wire UI or auto-call on reinstall |
| **P1** | No index on `payments(restaurant_id, bill_id)` | V7 | Add for report queries |
| **P1** | No `ON DELETE RESTRICT` on `restaurant_terminal` used in bills | V26 | Add or document soft-delete-only policy |

|--------|-----------|----------|---------|

**Scheduling:**
- **Periodic:** `MasterSyncWorker.schedule()` called from `KhanaBookApplication.onCreate()` using `ExistingPeriodicWorkPolicy.KEEP` with unique name `MasterSyncWorker`
- **One-time on network reconnect:** `enqueueMasterSyncOnce()` called from `MainActivity` when `NetworkMonitor` reports `ConnectionStatus.Available`

**WorkManager configuration:**
- Custom `HiltWorkerFactory` set via `Configuration.Provider` in `KhanaBookApplication`
- WorkManager auto-initialization disabled in manifest (custom configuration)

- **OWNER**: `Business Dashboard`, `Orders`, `Menu`, `Staff`, `Devices`
