Responsive: hamburger menu below 1024px with off-screen sidebar + backdrop overlay.

---

### 11. APP COMPONENT (app.component.ts)

Simple shell: `<router-outlet />` + `<app-global-toast />`

---

### 12. API STATE COMPONENT (core/components/api-state.component.ts)

A generic loading/error/retry wrapper (`<app-api-state>`) documented as "FIX #10" — but **not actually used by any page**. All pages implement their own loading/error patterns inline.

---

### 13. ISSUES / INCOMPLETE FEATURES FOUND

#### **Critical: Orphaned Page**
- **`MarketplaceSetupPageComponent`** (`pages/marketplace-setup/marketplace-setup-page.component.ts`) — a fully built 405-line page with Easebuzz settlement onboarding display, Zomato/Swiggy API key management with toggle switches, and save functionality. **It has NO route defined** in `app.routes.ts`. It is referenced nowhere in the sidebar navigation. It is completely inaccessible from the UI.

#### **Unused API Methods**
- **`recoverTerminal()`** in `business-api.service.ts` — the API call exists, the `RecoverTerminalRequest` model exists, but **no component ever calls this method**.

#### **OCR Menu Import is Read-Only Preview**
- In `MenuPageComponent` (line 292-293): *"Importing into the live menu happens on the Android POS app (sync). This web preview is read-only for v1."* — The OCR extraction shows a preview but cannot push to live menu.

#### **Business Suspended Error is Silently Swallowed**
- In `jwt.interceptor.ts` line 50: When `err.error?.error === 'BUSINESS_SUSPENDED'`, the 403 error is silently suppressed (no toast shown). The page just gets an error response with no user feedback.

#### **No Lazy Loading**
- Despite `AGENTS.md` mentioning lazy loading via `loadComponent`, all routes eagerly import components directly.

#### **No Chart/Visualization Library**
- Dependencies include only Angular core, rxjs, zone.js, and tslib. No charting library (Chart.js, D3, etc.) — all data displayed in stat cards and tables.

#### **`ApiStateComponent` is Defined but Not Used**
- The component exists at `core/components/api-state.component.ts` and is designed as a shared loading/error/retry wrapper, but **no page template uses `<app-api-state>`**. Each page implements its own loading/error pattern.

#### **Google GSI Script Hardcoded in index.html**
- `https://accounts.google.com/gsi/client` is loaded with `async defer` in `<head>`. The Google client ID is in both environment files (dev and prod share the same ID).

---

### 14. SUMMARY OF ALL FEATURES BY ROLE

#### **KBOOK_ADMIN (Super Admin) — 2 pages**
1. **Platform Dashboard** — stats grid (total businesses, live storefronts, staff, orders, revenue, refunded orders/amount) + suggestion cards
2. **Businesses Directory** — searchable/sortable/paginated table with suspend/activate, detail panel with revenue/GST/timezone

#### **OWNER (Business Owner) — 5 pages**
1. **Business Dashboard** — KPIs (total/today revenue, refunds, POS orders, pending payments, staff/menu count) + date range filter + recent orders table + setup confirmation checks (website, printer, kitchen printer, marketplace, staff/menu baseline) + next-step suggestions + order detail modal
2. **Orders** — filterable/paginated table with search, status, source, date range + CSV export + order detail modal + manual refund modal
3. **Menu** — filterable/paginated table with search, stock status, availability + add/edit/delete items modal + optimistic availability toggle + OCR menu import (PDF/image, read-only preview)
4. **Staff** — filterable/paginated table with search, role, status + create staff (with temporary password display) + edit staff + deactivate staff with self-protection
5. **Devices & Terminals** — terminal list with rename/deactivate/reactivate + device request queue with approve/reject

#### **SHOP_ADMIN — 1 page**
1. **Devices & Terminals** (owns page, same component, shared route)

#### **Unauthenticated Users**
1. **Login** — Google sign-in + email/phone + password login + full forgot password flow (phone → OTP → new password → success)

#### **Limited Access**
1. **Limited Access Page** — shown to users with unsupported roles (legacy roles)

## 2. ALL SERVICE FILES AND KEY METHODS

### 2.1 Core Sync Services (Interfaces + `GenericSyncService`)

| File | Key Methods |
|------|------------|
| `AuthService` | `login()`, `signup()`, `googleLogin()`, `requestSignupOtp()`, `requestPasswordResetOtp()`, `resetPassword()`, `checkUserExists()` |
| `AuthServiceImpl` | Implements all auth; creates restaurant+user on signup; checks business suspension |
| `UserService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()`, `requestMobileNumberUpdateOtp()`, `confirmMobileNumberUpdate()` |
| `RestaurantProfileService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()`, `incrementAndGetCounters()` |
| `CategoryService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()` |
| `MenuItemService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()` |
| `ItemVariantService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()` |
| `BillService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()` (3 overloads, terminal-scoped) |
| `BillItemService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()` |
| `BillPaymentService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()` |
| `StockLogService` | `pushData()`, `pullData()` |
| `GenericSyncService` | `handlePushSync()` — central sync engine; resolves relational IDs, enforces terminal ownership, cross-tenant guards, dedup gateway payments, bill number conflict validation, merge counter state |

### 2.2 Infrastructure Services

| File | Key Methods / Features |
|------|----------------------|
| `PasswordResetOtpService` | OTP generation, validation (4-digit or 6-digit), **WhatsApp OTP delivery via Meta Cloud API**, cleanup expired OTPs (scheduled every hour), supports: signup, password-reset, mobile-update, web-admin-password-reset flows |
| `WebAdminPasswordResetService` | Request/verify/reset password for web admin with temp token (10min TTL), cleanup expired temp tokens (every 10 min) |
| `AssetStorageService` | Upload/delete restaurant logos; converts to WebP via cwebp (`-lossless` for logos); versioned filenames; deletes old versions |
| `TokenBlocklistCleanupService` | Scheduled cleanup of expired JWT entries every hour |
| `SecurityAuditService` | Records security events (terminal activation, transfers, rejections, sync violations, refunds) |
| `TerminalManagementService` | Central terminal lifecycle: create requests, approve (pessimistic lock, 5-terminal limit), reject, deactivate, recovery/reclaim, rename, series allocation (A-Z, T1-Tn) |

### 2.3 Rate Limiters

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `LoginRateLimiter` | Per-IP rate limiting on login endpoints (Bucket4j) |
| `OtpRateLimiter` | Per-phone rate limiting on OTP requests (Bucket4j) |

### 2.4 Web Admin Business Services

| File | Key Methods / Features |
|------|----------------------|
| `AdminReadService` | Super-admin dashboard summary, list businesses, get business detail |
| `AdminWriteService` | Suspend/activate businesses |
| `BusinessReadService` | Owner dashboard (date filterable), marketplace setup, orders, order detail, menu, categories, staff, manual refunds, marketplace config |

### 2.5 Async Workers

| File | Key Methods / Features |
|------|----------------------|
| `MenuExtractionWorker` | Async menu PDF extraction using **Tabula** (PDF table extraction) + **PDFBox**; parses item/price/variant columns; stores extracted JSON |

## 3. COVERED & OUTSTANDING FEATURES

### 3.1 SMS/Email Sending
- **SMS**: No SMS integration found. Only OTP via **WhatsApp Cloud API** (Meta).
- **Email**: No email sending integration found. `email_invoice_consent` column exists in schema but no actual email delivery service.

### 3.2 File Upload / Storage
- **Menu extraction uploads** — stored in `uploads/` directory (configurable via `storage.upload-dir`)
- **Restaurant logo** — uploaded, converted to WebP via `cwebp`, stored in CDN path (`/var/www/cdn.kbook.iadv.cloud/restaurants/{id}/logo_v{version}.webp`)

### 3.3 PDF Generation
- **No server-side PDF generation**. The `InvoiceController` generates **HTML invoices** (not PDFs). These are served as public web pages.

### 3.4 Report Generation
- **No server-side report generation** (no JasperReports, no PDF/Excel reports). The web admin endpoints (`/business/dashboard`) compute stats in-memory from DB queries.

### 3.5 Scheduler Tasks
| Task | Schedule | Purpose |
|------|----------|---------|
| `PasswordResetOtpService.cleanupExpiredOtps()` | Every 1 hour | Delete expired OTP requests |
| `TokenBlocklistCleanupService.cleanupExpiredTokens()` | Every 1 hour | Delete expired JWT entries from blocklist |
| `WebAdminPasswordResetService.cleanupExpiredTokens()` | Every 10 min | Clean expired temp password-reset tokens |

### 3.6 Webhook Handlers
- **Zomato/Swiggy webhooks**: The `MarketplaceConfigController` references webhook URLs at `/api/v1/webhooks/zomato` and `/api/v1/webhooks/swiggy`, and webhook secrets are stored in `RestaurantProfile.zomatoWebhookSecret`/`swiggyWebhookSecret`. **However, NO actual webhook controller/endpoint exists yet** — the `marketplace_orders` and `marketplace_order_items` tables exist (created by V21), but there are no webhook handler classes in the codebase.
- **Easebuzz webhooks**: The `easebuzz_webhook_events` table exists (from V6), and `payment_webhook_logs` table (from V7). **No actual webhook handler endpoint** found in the controllers.

### 3.7 Admin Endpoints
Full super-admin suite exists at `/admin/**`:
- Dashboard summary (total businesses, live businesses, total staff, total orders, revenue, refunds)
- List all businesses (with owner, staff count, menu count, order count)
- Business detail
- Suspend/activate business

### 3.8 Customer Storefront
- **Not implemented server-side.** V8 created `customer_orders` and `customer_order_items` tables, and `RestaurantProfile` has `own_website_enabled` field. However, no storefront controllers or services exist.
- The `BusinessMarketplaceSetupResponse` has `paymentManagedByAdmin(true)` and `subMerchantStatus(null)` — setup is stubbed.

### 3.9 Marketplace (Zomato/Swiggy)
- **Config storage**: Full support for storing Zomato/Swiggy API keys, outlet/store IDs, webhook secrets, enable flags in `RestaurantProfile`
- **Config management**: `/business/marketplace/config` endpoints for read/write
- **Database tables**: `marketplace_orders`, `marketplace_order_items` (relate to `bills`)
- **Missing**: Actual webhook handler controllers, order ingestion from Zomato/Swiggy, order status sync back to platforms
- `Bill.sourceChannel` column tracks whether a bill came from Zomato, Swiggy, own_website, or POS

### 3.10 Payment Gateway (Easebuzz)
- **Database tables**: `restaurant_payment_config` (per-restaurant gateway config), `payments` (payment records), `payment_webhook_logs`, `easebuzz_webhook_events`
- **Config**: Easebuzz credentials abstracted to `restaurant_payment_config` table with encrypted salt
- **Tracking**: `bill_payments.gateway_txn_id`, `payments` table tracks refunds (refund_mode, refund_status, refund_amount, refund_arn_number, etc.)
- **Missing**: Actual Easebuzz payment initiation controller, payment callback/webhook handler

### 3.11 Multi-Device / Terminal Lifecycle
- **Fully implemented**: Terminal activation (first device auto-approves for OWNER, subsequent require approval), device registration requests (PENDING→APPROVED/REJECTED), recovery, reclaim, deactivation, reactivation, rename, transfer, credential rotation (version-based JWT revocation)
- **5-terminal limit** enforced atomically with pessimistic DB locks
- **SHOP_ADMIN role** can manage terminals but cannot push sync data or manage staff/menu

### 3.12 Business Suspension
- Implemented via `is_suspended` column on `restaurantprofiles`
- Suspended businesses are blocked at JWT filter level — all API calls return 403 "BUSINESS_SUSPENDED"
- Super-admin can suspend/activate via `/admin/businesses/{id}/suspend` | `/activate`

### 3.13 Menu Extraction (OCR)
- Upload PDF/images → async Tabula extraction → extracted JSON stored in `menu_extraction_jobs`
- Supports PDF, JPG, JPEG, PNG (max 10MB)
- Async via `@Async("menuExtractionExecutor")` with 4-10 thread pool

### 3.14 Public Invoice Pages
- Two HTML invoice endpoints (pre-finalize and finalized) with bill branding, payment status badges, review URL CTA, print CSS
- Secured via UUID public tokens (`public_token` column on bills)

### 3.15 Security Features
- **JWT auth** with device binding and IP allowlisting for KBOOK_ADMIN
- **Token revocation** via blocklist table + in-memory cache
- **Terminal tokens** with credential version (immediate revocation on recovery/deactivation)
- **Password reset token invalidation** — all existing JWTs become invalid
- **Security audit log** (`security_audit_log` table) — tracks terminal operations, sync violations, refunds
- **Rate limiting** on login (per IP) and OTP (per phone) via Bucket4j
- **Admin IP allowlist** — KBOOK_ADMIN restricted to configured IPs
- **Business suspension check** at JWT filter level
- **Content Security Policy** headers configured
- **Referrer Policy** headers configured
- **HSTS** with subdomains enabled

### 3.16 DevOps / Infra
- **Dockerfile**: Multi-stage build (Maven build → JRE runtime), Alpine-based, healthcheck on `/actuator/health/liveness`
- **docker-compose.yml**: Server-only stack (prod config, connects to external postgres)
- **docker-compose.production.yml**: Full stack (PostgreSQL 16 + server, bridge network, healthchecks)
- **Actuator**: health, info (git commit), metrics, prometheus endpoints
- **SpringDoc/OpenAPI**: Swagger UI available (disabled in production by default)
- **Prometheus metrics**: Via `micrometer-registry-prometheus`

---

## 4. DATABASE MIGRATION SUMMARY (V1–V42)

| Migration | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| **V1** | **Initial schema**: Creates 10 tables — `users`, `restaurantprofiles`, `categories`, `menuitems`, `itemvariants`, `bills`, `bill_items`, `bill_payments`, `stock_logs`, `menu_extraction_jobs`, `otp_requests`, `token_blocklist`. Adds FK constraints, CHECK constraints, and performance indexes. |
| **V2** | Adds kitchen printer config fields to `restaurantprofiles` (`kitchen_printer_enabled`, `kitchen_printer_name`, `kitchen_printer_mac`, `kitchen_printer_paper_size`) |
| **V3** | Tenant-scoped FK hardening: replaces all FK constraints with composite `(restaurant_id, id)` FKs; cleans orphaned cross-tenant references; adds tenant-scoped unique indexes |
| **V4** | Identity uniqueness hardening: normalizes emails to lowercase; adds case-insensitive unique indexes on `login_id`, `google_email`, `whatsapp_number` |
| **V5** | Menu item name uniqueness: partial unique index on `(restaurant_id, category_id, lower(trim(name)))` where not deleted |
| **V6** | Easebuzz payment gateway: adds `easebuzz_*` columns to `restaurantprofiles`, `gateway_txn_id`/`gateway_status`/`verified_by` to `bill_payments`, creates `easebuzz_webhook_events` table |
| **V7** | Backend-owned payments: creates `restaurant_payment_config` (gateway credentials per restaurant), `payments` (transaction records), `payment_webhook_logs` tables |
| **V8** | Customer storefront: creates `customer_orders` and `customer_order_items` tables |
| **V9** | Removes Easebuzz credential columns from `restaurantprofiles` (moved to `restaurant_payment_config`) |
| **V10** | Adds performance indexes: `bills(restaurant_id, daily_order_id)`, `customer_orders(restaurant_id, order_status)` |
| **V11** | Fixes date column: backfills `last_reset_date_proper` from VARCHAR, enforces NOT NULL. Adds encrypted_salt validation CHECK constraint |
| **V12** | Collapses legacy user roles: converts MANAGER/CASHIER/KITCHEN → OWNER |
| **V13** | Adds `refund_amount` column to `bills`, backfills cancelled+paid bills |
| **V14** | Payment refund tracking: adds 8 refund columns to `payments` table (refund_mode, refund_status, refund_amount, refund_reason, merchant_refund_id, refund_gateway_refund_id, refund_arn_number, refund_requested_at, refund_processed_at) |
| **V15** | Adds 'easebuzz' as distinct payment_mode in `bill_payments` CHECK constraint |
| **V16** | Backfills 'easebuzz' payment_mode where verified_by='easebuzz' (upi→easebuzz, part_cash_upi→part_cash_easebuzz, part_upi_pos→part_easebuzz_pos) |
| **V17** | Adds refund gateway observability columns to `payments`: `refund_last_gateway_payload`, `refund_last_gateway_sync_at` |
| **V18** | CDN asset storage: adds `logo_url`, `upi_qr_url`, `logo_version`, `upi_qr_version`, `invoice_footer` to `restaurantprofiles` |
| **V19** | Adds `public_token` (UUID) to `bills` for secure invoice URLs |
| **V20** | Adds marketplace fields: `zomato_outlet_id`, `swiggy_store_id`, `marketplace_notes` to `restaurantprofiles` |
| **V21** | Marketplace integration: adds `zomato_api_key`, `zomato_webhook_secret`, `swiggy_api_key`, `swiggy_webhook_secret` to `restaurantprofiles`. Creates `marketplace_orders` and `marketplace_order_items` tables with FKs |
| **V22** | Bill number uniqueness hardening: creates unique indexes on `(restaurant_id, lifetime_order_id)` and `(restaurant_id, last_reset_date, daily_order_id)` (behind duplicate guards) |
| **V23** | Dedup bill payments gateway_txn: partial unique index on `bill_payments(gateway_txn_id)` where not blank and not deleted; collapses pre-existing duplicates |
| **V24** | Adds `order_payment_flow_mode` (VARCHAR, default 'pay_before_food') to `restaurantprofiles` |
| **V25** | Adds `source_channel` column to `bills`; backfills from payment_mode for zomato/swiggy/own_website |
| **V26** | Multi-device invoice identity: adds `terminal_series`, `financial_year`, `invoice_series`, `invoice_sequence`, `invoice_number` to `bills`. Makes `lifetime_order_id` nullable. Creates `restaurant_terminal` table. Creates series-aware uniqueness indexes. Drops V22 legacy indexes. |
| **V28** | Bill terminal visibility/ownership: adds `created_terminal_id`, `created_device_id`, `current_owner_terminal_id` to `bills`. Backfills from existing data. Adds terminal-scoped indexes. |
| **V29** | Creates `security_audit_log` table for tracking security events |
| **V40** | Terminal identity sync fields: adds `terminal_name` and `is_active` to `restaurant_terminal`. Adds `terminal_id` column to all sync entity tables. Backfills terminal_id from terminal_series. Adds terminal-scoped bill index. |
| **V41** | Terminal lifecycle + device requests: adds `status` and `credential_version` to `restaurant_terminal`. Creates `device_registration_request` table with status lifecycle (PENDING/APPROVED/REJECTED/EXPIRED). Unique partial index on pending requests. |
| **V42** | Business suspension: adds `is_suspended` to `restaurantprofiles` with index |

|------|------|---------|

| `application.properties` | `server/src/main/resources/application.properties` | Main config: 8081 port, `/api/v1` context, PostgreSQL, HikariCP (20 pool), Flyway, JWT (30d expiry), actuator, multipart 10MB, CDN paths, Tomcat limits |

| `application-prod.properties` | `server/src/main/resources/application-prod.properties` | Structured JSON logging (ECS), CORS, prod Tomcat tuning (200 threads, 10K connections), compression, no Swagger |

## SUMMARY: COMPLETE SERVER FEATURE SET

1. **Multi-tenant SaaS POS backend** — JWT-authenticated, restaurant-scoped data isolation
2. **Offline-first sync engine** — push/pull for 9 entity types (profiles, users, categories, menu items, variants, bills, bill items, bill payments, stock logs); device-local IDs mapped to server IDs
3. **Authentication** — Phone+password login, Google Sign-In, OTP-based signup, password reset
4. **Multi-device terminal management** — Terminal activation (auto for first device, approval-gated for subsequent), recovery, reclaim, deactivation, reactivation, rename, transfer; 5-terminal limit; credential version rotation
5. **Role-based access** — OWNER, SHOP_ADMIN, KBOOK_ADMIN roles with granular endpoint permissions
6. **WhatsApp OTP delivery** — Via Meta Cloud API for signup, password reset, mobile update, web admin forgot password
7. **Invoice serving** — Public HTML invoice pages with payment status badges, print CSS, review CTAs
8. **Menu extraction (OCR)** — Upload PDF/image menus, async extraction via Tabula library
9. **Logo/CDN asset management** — Upload restaurant logos, WebP conversion via cwebp, versioned storage
10. **Easebuzz payment gateway** — Gateway credentials, payment records, refund tracking (tables exist; controller stubs missing)
11. **Zomato/Swiggy marketplace integration** — Config storage, API keys, webhook secrets, marketplace order tables (tables exist; webhook handlers missing)
12. **Customer storefront** — Tables exist (`customer_orders`, `customer_order_items`); no server implementation yet
13. **Web admin API** — Super-admin dashboard, business management (list, detail, suspend/activate); Owner dashboard (stats with date range, orders, staff, menu CRUD, refunds, terminal management)
14. **Security audit logging** — All terminal operations, sync violations, and manual refunds logged
15. **Rate limiting** — Login attempts (per IP) and OTP requests (per phone) via Bucket4j
16. **Business suspension** — Super-admin can suspend/activate businesses; suspended businesses blocked at filter level
17. **Schema migration** — 34 Flyway migrations covering the full schema evolution
18. **Monitoring** — Actuator health/liveness/readiness probes, Prometheus metrics, git info via `/actuator/info`
19. **Docker deployment** — Multi-stage Dockerfile, production docker-compose with PostgreSQL
20. **Public invoice pages** — Token-gated customer invoice view with full branding, tax display, and payment status
</task_result>
